Rica Aiza Cruz Ronald Villa T2 XL - Gradebook NaN NaN 50195850 INC0475294 2024-08-21 10:49:53 2024-08-21 12:56:40 MyLab Math - Grades not syncing 3PL Product Escalation 3PL_1.3, 3PL_FAD, 3PL_GS Ben Lethlean #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS,\n1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS\n2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS.\n\nPlease make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation. NaN Veronica Cavara NaN 50723660 INC0518679 2024-10-04 06:03:08 2024-10-04 23:22:20 Mastering Biology - Student Late Penalty Mastering Product Escalations incorrect_score, MX_MPU, PR_FAD Tana Regan This is expected behavior in Mastering Platform Update. The original due date for the assignment was September 24th; however, the instructor applied individual student settings to the assignment (I suspect after the student completed it) to give this student a due date October 3rd. Unlike legacy Mastering, Mastering Platform Update does not automatically regrade student submissions when a new due date is applied. For the new settings to apply to the student's submission, the student needs to reopen the assignment. Since the new due date has passed, the instructor will need to push it out to any time in the future, and then the student will need to reopen and save the assignment before the new due date passes.

Michael Pan T3 TL T3 NaN NaN NaN 50558734 INC0500673 2024-09-17 01:49:56 2024-09-17 04:17:09 MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working) Mastering Product Escalations MX_MPU, PR_FAD Tana Regan Hi Michael,\nIt sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided.
